▶ shopee-shipping-fee-claim — skill built + dry-run + FULL 27-shop sweep (270 raw / ~259 unique COM IDs, RM 16,248 at stake Apr15-May14) (19/5) 2026-05-19 MYT · skill + config + state + bat + scheduler setup · full 27-shop sweep 0 errors · webform DOM mapped · 7 spec corrections + 3 tuning improvements applied shopee-shipping-fee-claim Completed

Brief: Built end-to-end automation for the monthly Shopee MY shipping-fee claim webform. Bot iterates every MY shop under Patricia profile 70 (via get_sig bridge), filters R/R cases where buyer reason is literally "I want to return item in original / sealed condition", scrapes all Request IDs across pages for the claim cycle, batches into chunks of ≤10, and auto-submits the Shopee help webform a0137b284d764ea2886332ef64701958. Cross-run dedupe via state.submitted_request_ids. Continue-on-error per shop, STOPs cleanly on session expiry, no screenshots/Excel/sheet.

Files created (5):
  • C:\Users\tessf\.claude\skills\shopee-shipping-fee-claim.md — 21.9 KB skill spec (PHASE 0-8 procedure + hard rules + data model + error handling + first-run capture checklist)
  • C:\Users\tessf\.claude\skills\shopee-shipping-fee-claim\config.json — 2.9 KB (mode toggle, AdsPower target, Shopee SC endpoints, filter placeholders for first-run capture, webform selectors placeholders, schedule meta, 11-shop seed list)
  • C:\Users\tessf\.claude\skills\shopee-shipping-fee-claim\state.json — 222 B (empty seed: first_run_done=false, no submitted IDs)
  • C:\Users\tessf\scripts\shopee-shipping-claim.bat — 10.8 KB (TASK_FIRED beacon, AdsPower pre-check 12×10s, Claude run, report-file verify, separate board-log step, failure-fallback board entry, RestartOnFailure exit code)
  • C:\Users\tessf\scripts\setup_shopee_shipping_claim_schedule.bat — 2.0 KB (one-time scheduler registration: schtasks /sc monthly /d 15 /st 10:30 + PowerShell Set-ScheduledTask for WakeToRun + RestartOnFailure 3×15min)
Hard rules baked in: max 10 Request IDs per webform submission; reason filter must literal-match (char-for-char); continue-on-error per shop; no auto-retry within same run (avoid double-submit); session-dead → STOP not silent-relogin; first_run_override gated by config.first_run_override=true AND today=2026-06-15, flips state.first_run_done after firing once.
Date logic: normal cycle = previous-month-15 → this-month-14. Special 15 Jun 2026 first run = TWO cycles (Apr 15-May 14 label 2026-04, May 15-Jun 14 label 2026-05) because last month was skipped.
CLAUDE.md updated: skill #26 added to numbered registry (after sg-gap-monitor).
Dry-run results (19/5 same session): Phase 0 ok — profile 70 launched (port 58095) + get_shop_list ok (29 shops, 27 MY). Phase 1 ok — DOM cascader dance failed (React refused synthesized events 3x) so PIVOTED to direct API + client-side text filter (no numeric reason_id exposed in cards anyway). Phase 2 smoke ok — MurahYa Apr15-May14 yielded 35 COM-Return-Refund matches in 1,059 R/R cases (3.3% hit rate, 27 pages × 40). Phase 5a ok — webform DOM mapped: 10 fixed numbered slots with per-slot Shopee modal (input + Cancel + Confirm disabled-until-filled), claim-month text input at top (format "Apr 2026"), Submit at bottom. No live submissions (dry_run mode).
7 spec corrections applied to skill .md (19/5):
  1. get_shop_list response shape is j.shops[] (root) not j.data.shops[]; region field is country lowercase "my" not region.
  2. No numeric reason_id exists in card schema — only request_reason_text (bilingual EN/MS). Strategy switched to CLIENT-SIDE text filter (startsWith("I want to return item in original / sealed condition") + request_solution_text === "Return Refund").
  3. Webform expects order_sn (14-char), NOT return_sn (15-char). Placeholder explicitly says "Please Input an 14 digit order SN". Form's "Return ID" label is misleading Shopee jargon. Data model corrected: row_request_id_field = "order_sn".
  4. Webform is NOT bulk-paste textarea — it's 10 fixed slots, each with a per-slot Shopee modal workflow (click "Manual input order SN" → modal → fill → Confirm × 10 → Submit).
  5. No shop selector on the webform — one batch CAN mix order_sns from multiple shops.
  6. Webform title is "RIOC & ITRR" (dual-purpose). For now we submit ONLY COM/RIOC cases per user spec; ITRR explicitly out-of-scope.
  7. order_sn.slice(0,6) decodes as YYMMDD of order creation — useful for cycle-bucket sanity check (same for return_sn.slice(0,6)).
Full 27-shop sweep (Apr 15-May 14, 0 errors): All 27 shops swept successfully. 270 raw COM Request IDs / ~259 unique after order_sn dedupe / RM 16,248.04 total claim value. Top contributors: Hiranai 101 IDs (RM 2,442.52), KarlMobel 40 IDs (RM 5,115.39), MurahYa 35 IDs (RM 3,463.10), ValueSnap 35 IDs (RM 1,432.58) — these 4 carry 78% of volume. 16/27 shops had 0 eligible. Highest single claim: KarlMobel order_sn 260426TQ2WE23V — RM 907.99. Full per-shop breakdown in shopee-shipping-claim-fullsweep-2026-05-19.md.
Real 15 Jun 2026 first-run projection (refined): 259 unique × 2 cycles = ~518 IDs ÷ 10/batch = ~52 batches. @ ~25 sec/batch + 7s pacing + ~15 min sweep = ~45 min total runtime (was ~2hr upper-bound; actual is much faster). Fits bat's 2-hour ExecutionTimeLimit comfortably.
3 tuning improvements added 19/5 (skill .md PHASE 2/3):
  1. Inter-page sleep 350ms → 500ms + exponential-backoff retry (2s/3.5s/5s) on error: 10004 rate-limit. Without pacing, KarlMobel silently truncated at page 9 of 29 (lost 70% of data) on first attempt.
  2. Early-exit when page-1 total === 0 — 13 of 27 shops had 0 R/R in cycle. Skipping pagination on those saves ~40s/run.
  3. Within-cycle dedupe by order_sn before batching — 11 of 270 raw IDs are duplicates (multi-product orders generate multiple R/R cards with same order_sn). Without dedupe, webform slots get wasted.

▶ checkttrating bat — fixed 3 silent-fail bugs (2 of 3 verified live, 1 still failing) + new "no-log-on-fail" bug found in manual test (18/5) 2026-05-18 MYT · TTRatingCheck_5PM Task Scheduler · only 1 successful run (8/4) in last 40 days · root cause: timestamp format + nested ERRORLEVEL + TT captcha hang · manual test 21:26 MYT: Bug 1+2 fixes confirmed, but claude.cmd still exits 1 in ~3 min for unknown reason; bat also fails to log its own failure checkttrating Partial

Brief: User asked "what's running in schedule" and noted TTRatingCheck "always didn't run as scheduled". Investigation found the bat had been silently failing daily for ~40 days, with the only successful scheduled run being the very first one on 8/4. Latest report file: 30/4 (and that was a manual, not scheduled, run). Live state at investigation: PID 44812 had been hung for 27+ minutes inside the AdsPower retry loop, spawning child PowerShell processes that returned nothing useful.

Bug 1 — broken PowerShell timestamp format: Get-Date -Format ''yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'' → PS parses `''` as empty string + bareword yyyy-MM-dd → "Cannot convert 'yyyy-MM-dd' to DateTime". for /f reads nothing → !TS! empty → every log line wrote [] since 9/4. Fix: use (Get-Date).ToString('yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss') — clean single-quote-inside-double-quote, no escape gymnastics.
Bug 2 — stale %ERRORLEVEL% inside nested IF: cmd parses compound if (...) at parse-time, so the inner if %ERRORLEVEL% used the OUTER block's pre-execution value — the inner PowerShell API-status check's exit code was being ignored. Masked AdsPower API failures as success. Fix: collapse both checks into a single PowerShell call that returns 0 only if process AND API both healthy.
Bug 3 — no TT session-expiry handling: skill instructs Claude to log into 13 TT seller accounts. When sessions expire (every few days), TT throws a slider puzzle captcha that requires a human drag (per feedback_tt_relogin_captcha_blocks_automation.md). claude.cmd waited indefinitely → bat never reached COMPLETED OK or FAILED → Task Scheduler's PT2H ExecutionTimeLimit + RestartCount=3 produced ~8 hours of hung processes per day. Fix: prompt now instructs Claude to detect expiry per shop (check location.href for /login|/passport or absent Shop Health widget within 10s), mark SESSION_EXPIRED, close browser, skip to next shop, leave that shop's row BLANK in the Google Sheet paste, and list SESSION_EXPIRED shops under "Manual re-login needed" in the report + board entry. Board result becomes partial if any shop expired, ok only when all 13 returned data.
Task Scheduler change: ExecutionTimeLimit PT2H → PT30M. RestartCount left at 3 (XML schema requires it when RestartInterval is set; new bat doesn't hang anymore so restarts won't fire on hang).

  • C:\Users\tessf\scripts\checkttrating.bat — rewrote with all 3 fixes (backup at checkttrating.bat.bak-2026-05-18).
  • C:\Users\tessf\.claude\skills\checkttrating.md — added explicit "🚨 SESSION-EXPIRY CHECK" step in Step 2 between Navigate and Dismiss popups.
  • schedule-log.txt — archived 78-line bloated log (all empty [] timestamps) to .bak-2026-05-18, replaced with single fix-note header line.

Worth a sweep tomorrow.

▶ Scheduler hardening — all 10 daily tasks now wake PC from sleep + catch up if missed + don't stop on battery (15/5) 2026-05-15 ~17:30 MYT · Updated 10 scheduled tasks (ParcelClaimAuto_945AM, TT_RR_Audit_10_15AM, ChatAudit_910AM, ClaudeSgGapMonitor, KinataOrderCheck_12PM/430PM, SBVariationAudit_930AM, ParcelSplitCrosscheck_1000AM, TTRatingCheck_5PM, BoardMirrorSync_10min) with WakeToRun=True + StartWhenAvailable=True + AllowOnBattery=True + DontStopOnBattery=True + RestartCount=3/5min. Plus fixed DC wake-timer policy (was DISABLED on battery, now “Important Wake Timers Only” same as AC). scheduler infra Completed

Brief: User concern “make sure all schedule run task run even if my pc off? especially parcelclaimauto.” Found mixed settings across 10 daily tasks. Hardened all of them so they fire from sleep/hibernate, catch up if missed, and survive battery-mode transitions.

Trigger: Direct user instruction at session close to make scheduler resilient to PC sleep/battery.
Before → After (per task):
  • ParcelClaimAuto_945AM: Wake T · Missed T · OnBat T · StopBat=False — was already mostly correct, added DontStopOnBattery + RestartCount=3 (5min interval)
  • TT_RR_Audit_10_15AM: Wake F→T · Missed T · OnBat T · StopBat=False (was StopBat=True) · RestartCount=0→3
  • ChatAudit_910AM: Wake T · Missed T · OnBat T · StopBat=False · RestartCount=3
  • ClaudeSgGapMonitor: Wake F→T · Missed F→T · OnBat F→T · StopBat F (was T) · RestartCount=3 (was 0). Critical — was failing exit 2147946720 today.
  • KinataOrderCheck_12PM & 430PM: Wake T · Missed T · OnBat T · StopBat=False. RestartCount stays 0 (Access denied on retry — task created with elevated rights, need admin powershell to set restart).
  • SBVariationAudit_930AM: Wake T · Missed T · OnBat T · StopBat=False · RestartCount=3
  • ParcelSplitCrosscheck_1000AM: Wake F→T · Missed T · OnBat F→T · StopBat F (was T) · RestartCount=3
  • TTRatingCheck_5PM: Wake T · Missed T · OnBat T · StopBat=False · RestartCount=3
  • BoardMirrorSync_10min: Wake F→T · Missed F→T · OnBat F→T · StopBat F (was T) · RestartCount=3
Power scheme fix: Wake timers on battery (DC mode) were set to 0 = Disabled — that means even with WakeToRun=True, tasks would NOT wake the laptop when running on battery. Changed to 2 = Important Wake Timers Only (same as AC mode). Applied via powercfg /setdcvalueindex SCHEME_CURRENT SUB_SLEEP RTCWAKE 2 + activated.
Sleep states supported: S0 Low Power Idle (Modern Standby) + Hibernate + Fast Startup. S1/S2/S3 not supported by firmware. All available sleep modes support wake timers.
⚠️ Critical limitation — PC fully OFF cannot be woken by Task Scheduler: If you press the power button to fully shut down the laptop, NO scheduled task can wake it. Windows Task Scheduler can only wake from Sleep/Standby or Hibernate — not from full shutdown. For PC-fully-off scenarios you would need either: (a) BIOS/UEFI “Wake on RTC Alarm” enabled (needs firmware-level setting, varies by laptop model), or (b) leave PC in Sleep mode overnight instead of Shutdown.
Result: ok — all 10 tasks now wake-resilient. PC asleep over weekend = tasks fire normally. PC plugged in OR on battery = tasks fire. Task fails once = auto-retry 3 times at 5min intervals. PC physically shut down = tasks queue and fire when you power back on (StartWhenAvailable=True). Most resilient short of enabling BIOS-level RTC wake.
FOLLOW-UP fix ~23:50 MYT (same session): ClaudeSgGapMonitor 9AM run today still failed exit 2147946720 (0x80070420 ERROR_SERVICE_ALREADY_RUNNING) despite earlier hardening — root cause was task setting MultipleInstancesPolicy=IgnoreNew. Changed to StopExisting via XML re-import (PowerShell enum doesn't expose StopExisting; used schtasks /Query /XML → sed-replace → schtasks /Delete + /Create /XML). Verified XML now shows <MultipleInstancesPolicy>StopExisting</MultipleInstancesPolicy>. NextRunTime preserved 16/5 9:00 AM. Other settings (WakeToRun/StartWhenAvailable/restart 3x5min/2hr timeout) preserved. Now any zombie instance gets killed before next run starts — prevents the IgnoreNew block.

▶ board cleanup — de-bloat + dedupe (AM 0af7c70) + alignment/title/tiktokrraudit fixes (PM 02a735d) 2026-05-11 ~15:55 + 17:30 MYT · AM: 72k→16.6k lines, fix 5/11 pc-auto entry, merge 4/27 dups · PM: fix wrapper-closes-early (2 stray </div>), entry-title width=0 (CSS), tiktokrraudit body orphan field · commits 0af7c70 + 02a735d board-maintenance Completed

Brief: User flagged the activity board as “cacat / messy / ugly / weird” with duplicate tasks. Audited index.html and found three concrete problems; fixed all in one commit.

Fix 1 — Whitespace bloat (root cause of “ugly” feel):
  • Source file had 6 blank lines between every line of content across head/style/body/entries. 72,039 total lines but only ~8,500 of actual content.
  • Browser ignores blank lines between tags, but <pre> blocks (2 instances on 5/7 + 5/5) rendered with huge vertical gaps — visible “ugly” symptom.
  • Collapsed all runs of 3+ newlines to a single blank line (in pre blocks: collapsed to no blank lines).
  • Result: 72,039 → 16,637 lines (4.3× reduction), 1,108,904 → 966,649 bytes (13% smaller payload). git diff for this change: +8,724 / −64,188.
Fix 2 — Broken 5/11 parcelclaim-auto entry:
  • That entry used an old <h3> header pattern instead of the consistent <div class="entry-summary"><span class="entry-title"> collapsible structure all other entries use. Chevron-collapse UI didn’t work on this entry — it always rendered expanded with a heading that didn’t match the rest.
  • Replaced the <h3> + first <div class="field"> wrapper with the standard summary block (chevron + title + meta + 2 tags) and wrapped the remaining content in <div class="entry-body">. Entry now collapses/expands consistently.
Fix 3 — 4/27 duplicates (12 entries → 6):
  • parcelclaim-auto: 3 entries (L61448 + L63424 + L65032) → merged into the most complete one with a “Merged duplicate entries” section listing the absorbed entries’ titles.
  • checkkinataorder: 3 entries (L63104 + L64704 + L65808) → merged 3 separate scheduled-run logs into one.
  • checksbvariation: 2 entries (L63936 + L65376) → merged into one (morning review + main 09:30 audit).
  • cs3 KarlMobel deep re-verify (L61216) was a sub-task of the chataudit weekend entry → folded as an inline note into the chataudit entry, separate entry deleted.
  • Other 6 entries on 4/27 (tiktokrraudit, csrrcredited, chataudit, the merged 3 above) preserved.
Why this keeps happening (analysis):
  • Whitespace bloat: introduced over time by past mcp__github__create_or_update_file calls where the literal content string accumulated extra newlines (likely from copy-paste through tools that double-newline). Each PUT preserved + added more. The fix here is one-time; future writes should normalize before push.
  • Inconsistent entry HTML: 5/11 parcelclaim-auto was added via a different code path than the rest (likely a manual paste using the older <h3> template before the entry-summary pattern became standard). Going forward: every new entry must use the entry-summary/entry-body wrappers.
  • 4/27 duplicates: that day had multiple runs of the same scheduled skill across the day (12PM + manual + 4:30PM kinata; AM dry_run + live + re-verification parcelclaim-auto; morning + evening sbvariation). Each run logged a separate entry instead of appending to the day’s existing entry. CLAUDE.md HARD RULE #4 (“strictly no duplicates — merge into existing entry for same date/skill”) was added in response and applies to all subsequent days.

PM follow-up — 3 layout bugs reported via screenshot (commit 02a735d):
  • Bug A: wrapper closes prematurely after filter-bar. Diagnosed via DOM inspection in AdsPower profile 70: document.body.children showed 11 day-group divs as direct siblings of .wrapper (should be children). wrapper.contains(firstEntry) === false. Root cause: 2 stray </div> tags inside the csrrcredited 5/6 entry (file lines 6449+6451) that survived the AM merge script. They auto-closed the wrapper at line 6455, leaving header+filter at 1224px while entries broke out to 1521px viewport width. The misalignment the user circled in red. Fix: wrote fix_unbalanced_entries.py that walks every entry, counts <div> opens vs </div> closes, and deletes the trailing extras. After fix: total file balance 934 == 934 (was 932 opens / 934 closes pre-fix). Wrapper now contains all entries.
  • Bug B: every entry-title rendered at width=0. Diagnosed: entry-meta had no dedicated CSS rule, so it inherited white-space:normal and grew to wrap content to 3-4 lines, while entry-title (flex:1; min-width:0; white-space:nowrap) collapsed to 0. The chevron + skill-pill + meta + tags showed, but the title text was invisible. Fix: added .entry-summary .entry-meta {flex:0 1 auto; max-width:42%; white-space:nowrap; overflow:hidden; text-overflow:ellipsis} and tightened .entry-title to flex:1 1 240px; min-width:200px. Result: titles now render 200-435px wide, meta truncates with ellipsis, entries collapse to clean 54px rows.
  • Bug C: 5/11 tiktokrraudit entry had a <div class="field"> orphan outside .entry-body. The “PM NEW-half sweep” block was a direct child of .entry instead of nested in .entry-body, so it rendered regardless of collapse state — visible as the awkward text hanging off the left side in the user’s screenshot. Cause: the AM <h3>-to-entry-summary fix on the 5/11 parcelclaim-auto entry inserted an extra </div> at a wrong line, which dragged the next field outside body. Fix: moved the field inside .entry-body and rebalanced closes. Confirmed: 0 entries with orphan fields across all 85 entries.
Diagnostic methodology (so this is repeatable):
  • Loaded local file:///C:/Users/tessf/board-patricia/index.html in AdsPower profile 70 (GitHub Pages not enabled on this repo).
  • Used getBoundingClientRect() on .wrapper, .filter-bar, .day-header, .entry — spotted the 1224px vs 1521px width mismatch.
  • Walked wrapper.children + document.body.children — confirmed day-groups had escaped the wrapper.
  • Wrote find_unbalance.py: line-by-line depth counter starting from <body>; pinpointed line 6455 as where depth first dropped to 0 (wrapper close).
  • Wrote fix_unbalanced_entries.py: per-entry <div> balance audit + deletion of trailing extras; verified file-level balance after.
  • For Bug B: used getComputedStyle on every .entry-summary child to compare flex properties — found meta was eating all space due to white-space:normal.
  • For Bug C: walked entry.children and checked which had class field directly (should be 0).
  • Sanity check after fix: clicked tiktokrraudit tab, verified 11 entries all 54px tall (collapsed), clicked one entry, verified body expanded with all fields nested correctly.

EVENING root-cause fix — pre-commit lint installed (commit 3f0f272):

User asked: “can avoid this to happened again by fixing the root cause?” Root cause of every visual bug today: no validation before edits hit index.html, so whitespace bloat / unbalanced divs / orphan fields / inconsistent <h3> entries / same-skill date-duplicates slipped through and only surfaced when eyeballing the rendered page.

Solution: .scripts/board_lint.py (~250 lines) + .git/hooks/pre-commit that runs it. Lint auto-fixes whitespace silently (re-stages cleaned file) and blocks commits on the 4 structural bug classes. CLAUDE.md auto-log section rewritten to require local-clone + git push workflow (so the hook always fires), and to require lint --check before any MCP create_or_update_file PUT (which bypasses the hook).

Lint check coverage:
  • Whitespace bloat — collapses 3+ newlines to 1 blank line; inside <pre> blocks collapses to 0 blank lines. AUTO-FIX + re-stage. Prevents recurrence of the 72k-lines / 1.1MB bloat seen this morning.
  • File-level <div> balance — total opens must equal total closes. Catches the stray-</div> bug that closed .wrapper at line 6455 and broke every entry out to 1521px viewport width this afternoon.
  • Per-entry balance — each <div class="entry"> block balances within its own range (catches stray closes earlier than file-level audit, with line numbers).
  • Entry structure — every entry must have entry-summary + entry-body. No <h3> headers (broken 5/11 parcelclaim-auto pattern). No <div class="field"> as direct child of .entry (the orphan-field bug from this afternoon's tiktokrraudit entry).
  • Same-date+same-skill duplicates — flags entries with same data-date and matching skill prefix in title. Strips leading “DD/M ” date prefixes so “30/4 csrrcredited” and “csrrcredited 30/4” classify the same way. Enforces HARD RULE #4 automatically instead of relying on memory.
Test harness: C:\Users\tessf\test_lint_bugs.py injects each bug class into a copy and confirms the lint catches it. All 5 PASS:
  • Bug 1 (unbalanced div): caught with message “937 opens vs 938 closes (diff +1)”.
  • Bug 2 (orphan field): caught with line number + “direct child of .entry, must be inside .entry-body”.
  • Bug 3 (<h3> entry): caught with “uses old <h3> header pattern instead of entry-summary”.
  • Bug 4 (duplicate): caught with both line numbers + skill name + “merge into one entry per CLAUDE.md HARD RULE #4”.
  • Bug 5 (whitespace): reported in --check mode (“would normalize, saving 8,511 bytes”), auto-fixed in default mode.
Bonus catches on first run against current file:

Calibration lesson (saved to feedback_chataudit_calibration_rules.md):
  • First pass too narrow: heuristic classifier only checked HOLDING_ONLY pattern (holding template + no dash-signoff agent reply). Missed wrong-info-with-signoff, no-agent-reply-when-no-holding-template, system-flagged messages, wrong-context replies. Per skill Section 4c, Q&A semantic check on every chat is MANDATORY but was skipped in the first pass.
  • Second pass too broad: flagged standard-policy answers as “misses” (Lucy 24h template for urgent requests is the correct shop-policy answer), flagged honest non-confirmation (helmet authenticity Q where shop genuinely doesn’t know SIRIM status), flagged customer-self-resolved cases (rifat143 just re-ordered), flagged already-replied cases the classifier missed.
  • Calibrated definition of a miss: (a) no agent reply when customer made substantive complaint, OR (b) wrong-info that contradicts product fact, OR (c) wrong-context reply, OR (d) Shopee-system-flagged message uninvestigated, OR (e) no human escalation on aged-stuck order. NOT a miss = standard-policy / honest-non-confirmation / customer-self-resolved / already-replied / Pattern A2 closer / comp negotiation respected / already in CS pipeline.
  • Future audits must do BOTH heuristic + Q&A semantic on every chat, AND cross-reference against the “IS NOT a miss” rules in the calibration memory before reporting.

Discoveries this session:
  • Webapp /api/sb-variation/{id} accepts PATCH (not /api/sb-variation directly — that returns 405). Single-field body works: {"buyerDecision": "Cancelled"}. Multi-field accepted (e.g. add csRemarks). Returns {"success":true,"affectedRows":1,"newValues":{...}}. Fields cancellation_check and contactSent return 400 "No valid fields" — not patchable via this endpoint.
  • TT Shop Chat URL: https://seller-my.tiktok.com/chat/inbox/current?lang=en-US&from=seller_center_navigation_im (NOT /im — "No matching route"). Search by Marketplace Order ID inside chat works for buyers who have an existing thread (open OR closed). Closed thread reopen worked cleanly via row click + textarea typing + Send button.
  • TT cannot initiate chat for buyers who never messaged the shop — only "Send updates" (templated shipment notification) is available pre-buyer-contact. Affects 101001, 101006 (and likely most NEW No Stock cases — buyer typically only chats post-shipment or post-delivery).
  • SiteGiant Order ID search: sitegiant.co/orders → switch "Order ID" dropdown to "Marketplace Order ID" via Ant Design selector (filterForm_selectedOption) → fill filterForm_searchValue input → Enter. Captures status + product + variation + buyer (masked) per row. Used for all 7 lookups today.
  • Lazada profile mapping: profile 82 = das.nature (NOT MurahYa). profile 81 = "CS Laz Murahya" (autofill login — click Login button only). profile 83 = Lovento (per 8/5 memory). Updates the config.json lazada_range: "81-83" map.

Paste flow into fbs_apr26 Google Sheet

Working method discovered: programmatic ClipboardEvent dispatch is blocked by Sheets (defaultPrevented:true on every variant tested). The trick that does work:

  1. Pipe TSV via Bash: cat tab_X.tsv | clip.exe (puts on Windows OS clipboard)
  2. Switch to target tab in Sheets, position to A1 via name box
  3. Trigger TRUSTED Ctrl+V via mcp__adspower__press-key with ControlLeft+v

Methodology notes:
  • AdsPower MCP unavailable; built chataudit_helper.py using requests + websocket-client (with suppress_origin=True to bypass Chrome 111+ origin check) talking to AdsPower-launched browsers via Chrome DevTools Protocol.
  • Each profile started via /api/v1/browser/start, connected to /devtools/page/<id>, ran JS via Runtime.evaluate with Page.bringToFront first to keep tab active (else document.hidden=true paused React virtualization scroll-load).
  • Scroll-load uses synthetic WheelEvent + scroll dispatch to trigger lazy-load (programmatic scrollTop alone doesn't trigger React-virtualized lazy-fetch).
  • Batches: 6 chats per evaluate call, 18s pause between batches. Per-chat panel retries 7×2.5s wait (cs4) or 4×1.8s (others).
  • Deep-verify: per-target re-open via search box / list click + verify panel startsWith(name) + HH:MM timestamp + length > 250.
